Withdraws from the International Parliamentary Conference

French Representative Firmly Refuses to Apologize

National News Agency, Geneva, 25th – French representative Reynaud at the International Parliamentary Union has firmly refused to apologize to Italy. The Italian delegation has announced its withdrawal from the conference. The chairman announced the letter from the Italian delegation at the meeting today, and then continued to discuss the issue of poisons, and then passed a resolution urging all countries participating in the conference to ratify the conventions related to the suppression of poisons.

Important News

North China Generals Arrive in Beiping 60

Han Fuju and Shang Zhen Arrive First

Xu Yongchang and Others Will Follow Soon

Beiping Correspondence: Recently, due to the tense situation in North China, senior generals have arrived in Beiping to discuss major plans together. Those who have already arrived include Han Fuju and Shang Zhen. The situation is as follows:

Han Fuju: Shandong Chairman Han Fuju and former 13th Route Commander-in-Chief Shi Yousan arrived in Beiping at 3:00 AM on the 23rd. According to Han's statement, "I (Han referring to himself) am a soldier and come from the ranks. As for the country, I only know to do my best in my duties. Also serving as civil administrator, the responsibility is heavy. In Shandong, the goal is to eliminate bandits and pacify the people. Now that foreign aggression is becoming increasingly urgent, I believe that (1) internally, we should implement unity and combine the strength of the whole country to resist foreign aggression. Naturally, there are ways. With the loss of the Northeast, national defense has been lost. The impact has made Tianjin and Beiping precarious. With the issue of Rehe arising, the people of the country must recognize that it is not the issue of Rehe, but the entire issue of China. Everyone must use their strength to help this national crisis. In North China, in particular, everyone should think of a way to unite sincerely. The adage 'lips are gone, teeth are cold' is self-evident. If the Japanese occupy this place, they will want that place. If everyone has the mindset that China is vast and rich in resources, then it will not end. Regarding this point, before leaving Jinan, I telegraphed Sun Chu, Yang Aiyuan, and Xu Yongchang in Shanxi, asking them to meet in Beiping to discuss solutions. I have received a reply telegram, agreeing to depart immediately. If time permits, they can come together, otherwise one or two of them will come along. Today's affairs are extremely urgent. Everyone must seek solutions in the absence of solutions, and seek survival in the face of impossibility. (2) As a soldier, I only know to protect the country and its borders. If foreigners invade our land, even an inch or a foot, I will never ignore it. Today, not only must the current situation be maintained, but the lost territories of the Northeast must also be recovered. China's nation raises the most soldiers. This is the day to serve the country. Although the enemy's special qualities are strong, if we use a prolonged method to extend the situation, in the end, justice can still triumph over power. Soldiers only need to be able to sacrifice, and they must sacrifice themselves. There is no reason why we cannot win the final victory. Life is only a hundred years, and everyone will eventually die. As long as we see through the meaning of death, nothing is unsacrificable, nothing is impossible to do. Today, against foreign countries, is precisely a great path to do. In short, China today is at a time of reckless courage, not a time to be afraid in the face of adversity. The people of the country should immediately realize that after the country is destroyed, there is no such thing as rich or poor, noble or lowly, all will perish together. (3) Shi Hanzhang came with me this time to meet with Director Zhang (Xueliang). It is a manifestation of sincere unity. Shi often says that he is from the Northeast, and now he has personally experienced the plight of a destroyed country, which is extremely painful. The only way to save it in the future is for everyone to unite and defend the country. Director Zhang is said to have a minor illness. After the adjutant-general Tang (Guozhen) makes contact, he will accompany him to pay respects to Director Zhang. Mr. Feng (Yuxiang) is currently in Taian, reading, writing, painting bamboo, and traveling, with a very leisurely attitude, and has no other intentions for the time being. I came here at the invitation of Director Zhang to discuss military and political issues. I plan to stay in Beiping for a week and then return to Shandong."

Shang Zhen: The 32nd Army Commander Shang Zhen arrived in Beiping by the Pinghan express train at 7:40 AM on the 23rd. Han Fuju, Wan Fulin, and Li Peiji welcomed him at the station. After Shang got off the train, he thanked the welcomers one by one and asked when Han had arrived in Beiping. He then took a car to his private residence on Nanchang Street to rest. The reporter went to Shang's residence to send a card requesting an audience, and obtained the following remarks: "A part of my army has been ordered to move defenses to Henan Province, and they have now arrived at the new defenses. Gao Hongwen's brigade is in western Henan, with the brigade headquarters stationed in Luoyang. Huang Guanghua's brigade is in northern Henan, with the brigade headquarters stationed in Zhengzhou. The 32nd Army Headquarters is stationed in Xingcun. The 42nd Brigade and all directly subordinate units are still stationed at the original defense in Shunde. After the relocation of the Gao and Huang brigades was completed, I went to Hankou on the 11th to pay respects to Chairman Chiang to report on the progress of the relocation. I stayed in Hankou for four days and five nights, and returned north to Shunde on the 16th. The communist bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui are scheduled to be eliminated within three months. Even if it is difficult to complete on schedule at that time, they should be wiped out within six months. Since Chairman Chiang arrived in Hankou, the morale of the army has been greatly boosted, and discipline has been greatly improved. I came here to pay respects to Director Zhang and report on the defense. I will stay in Beiping for three to five days and then return to the defense area."

Xu Yongchang: Shanxi Provincial Government Chairman Xu Yongchang sent a telegram to Han Fuju on the 23rd, saying that he would definitely come to Beiping from Taiyuan on the 25th or 26th, with one of Yang Aiyuan and Sun Chu accompanying him. In addition, Suiyuan Chairman Fu Zuoyi will also come to Beiping in the next few days to pay respects to Director Zhang and discuss military and political issues in North China. (24th)

He Yingqin Reports on Resisting Aggression and Suppressing Bandits 61

He Yingqin reported on resisting aggression and suppressing bandits at the Central Memorial Week on the 25th morning, stating roughly that the important issues facing China currently are resisting aggression and suppressing bandits. Failure to resist foreign aggression will lead to national subjugation, and failure to suppress the Red bandits will lead to racial extinction. I am responsible for suppressing bandits in Jiangxi Province, and I will now report on the recent bandit situation in various provinces in general terms: (1) Jiangxi Province: Jiangxi is the base of the Red bandits, and the extent of the bandit disaster and the difficulty of suppression are the greatest among all provinces. It is estimated that the bandits have an organized military force of over ten armies, approximately 50,000 to 60,000 men, with approximately 30,000 to 40,000 rifles. They are scattered in southern Jiangxi, including Xingguo, Yudu, Ruijin, Shicheng, Ningdu; western Jiangxi, including Lianhua, Yongxin, Xiushui, Tonggu; eastern Jiangxi, including Geyang, Dexing; western Fujian, including Changting, Jianning; the border between Guangdong and Jiangxi, including Dayu, Nanxiong; and the border between Hunan and Jiangxi, including Guidong, Rucheng. In the past, methods of suppressing bandits that sought quick results consumed much effort but achieved little success. This time, the method of suppressing bandits is to take a steady and solid approach. After recovering a place, the area is thoroughly cleared. Since implementing this approach, the bandit units in eastern Jiangxi, such as Fang Shao, and western Jiangxi, such as Kong Duan, have been dealt severe blows repeatedly. The Peng Dehuai bandit unit, which has been causing trouble on the border between Jiangxi and Hunan, has also been encircled and attacked by the combined forces of the National Army from Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Hunan in the area around Guidong, Rucheng, Jilongyingqian, and Shangbao. The Peng bandits, failing to invade Hunan, and the Zhu bandits also fled back to Jiangxi from Fujian, attempting to reoccupy their old nest in southern Jiangxi and plotting to disturb the border of Guangdong. However, the Guangdong army under Yu Hanmou was prepared, and the troops from Hunan and Jiangxi continued to pursue them relentlessly. Recently, Zhang Meixin's division of my unit defeated the bandits near Nanxiong. The 19th Route Army has now fully arrived in Fujian, and Chen Bonan has increased the number of troops and the Gui army under Wang Zanbin are successively concentrating on the border of Jiangxi. A major blow to the Red bandits and the annihilation of all or most of them is inevitable soon. The reports from Hong Kong that Dayu, Nanxiong, and Nankang have been captured by the bandits are completely untrue. (2) The border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui: The border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, including Huang'an, Luotian, Yingshan, Shangcheng, northern Huang'an and Macheng, western Liu'an and Huoshan, southern Guangshan, Luoshan, Huangchuan, Gushi, and southeastern Xinyang, spans hundreds of miles, with a bandit gathering of 30,000 men and approximately 20,000 rifles. The bandit leaders are Ji Xun, Duan Dechang, Xu Xiangqian, and others. Although various armies have been suppressing them for years, the bandits are constantly on the move, making it difficult to eliminate them. Last month, taking advantage of our engagement with foreign affairs, the bandits advanced to Gushi with a portion of their forces and fled to the area of Sanhejian, Liu'an, and Huoqiu with the majority of their forces. They even occupied Zhengyangguan for a time, and the Jinpu Railway line became strained. Subsequently, Commander-in-Chief Chiang went to Wuhan to supervise the suppression, and the Central reinforcements arrived. Huoqiu has been recovered by Xu's division, and the Red bandits have suffered over 7,000 casualties and prisoners. The future of suppressing bandits in the border area of the three provinces should improve day by day. (3) Hubei Province: In Hubei Province, apart from the three towns of Wuhan and their surrounding areas, famine victims and bandits are mixed everywhere. In addition to eastern Hubei, central Hubei has He Duan with approximately 30,000 men and 20,000 rifles. Southern and western Hubei have Kong Hechong, Wang Bingnan, and a portion of He Duan's forces, with approximately 10,000 men and approximately 5,000 rifles. To the north, there are Chen Kechun, Wei Guozhu, and other bandit groups with 20,000 men and approximately 10,000 rifles, relying on the mountains and lakes, and constantly on the move. In the spring of this year, He Chengjun divided the entire province into three pacification zones and made efforts to clear out the bandits. Xu Yuanquan's troops in central Hubei and Wang Lingji's Sichuan army in western Hubei have achieved results, inflicting significant blows on the bandits. Now Chiang is in Wuhan, planning a comprehensive clearing. Although the bandit problem in Hubei is deep-rooted, it should not be difficult to eliminate them together with the bandits in the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui at an early date. The Red bandits in various provinces are holding up more than 600,000 National Army troops. While major Red bandit forces must be destroyed and cleared by military force, the root of the problem still lies in political improvement and transportation construction. In early May, the Jiangxi Provincial Bandit Suppression

Meeting was held, and I proposed ten motions: (1) Strictly implement the Baojia system (household registration); (2) Organize the masses; (3) Build fortresses extensively; (4) Promote highways; (5) Clean up land; (6) Recruit refugees; (7) Comfort and appease those who were coerced into joining; (8) Assist in the clearing of bandits; (9) Promote cooperation; (10) Clarify official corruption. All were passed. Chiang also convened a bandit suppression meeting in Lushan, and after extensive consultation and inquiry on administrative construction issues related to bandit suppression, a perfect decision was made, strictly ordering the provinces in the bandit areas to follow and implement it. The Lushan meeting also decided on the principles for dealing with those who have reformed and those who were coerced into becoming bandits: (1) If the masses were indeed coerced, they should first submit a pledge that they were indeed coerced in the past and that they will sincerely reform in the future, and the pledge should be guaranteed by their father, brother, clan head, or a fair-minded local gentry, and the pledge should be submitted to the county magistrate for approval. (2) Those who were coerced into joining the bandits and have reformed after being approved by the county should be ordered to have guarantors to monitor and correct their behavior at any time. (3) If the reformed elements voluntarily return to their hometowns and have not held important false positions or committed major crimes, they should voluntarily issue a sincere pledge of repentance and attach a guarantee from their father, brother, and five neighbors, and submit it to the county magistrate for approval. (4) After the reformed elements are approved by the county magistrate, the county magistrate will issue a certificate of reformation, and they should be supervised by the guarantor at any time. (5) Reformed elements who can demonstrate one of the following achievements in bandit suppression work may be exempted from the restrictions of the preceding article and may be separately submitted to the county magistrate for review and award according to their circumstances: (A) Capturing and delivering bandit leaders; (B) Reporting the hidden area of bandit leaders or a huge bandit den and leading the way to its destruction; (C) Surrendering a number of guns or a large amount of grain;

(D) Being able to publicly expose all the inhuman crimes and rebellious acts of the Red bandits in the place of residence, with notable achievements. (6) The lives and property of the coerced masses and reformed elements should be fully protected after being approved by the competent government agency to return to their place of residence. (7) Local people should not satirize or insult the coerced masses and reformed elements who have been approved by the government to return to their place of residence. (8) Any public officials who handle the reformation and cause extortion or obstruct the reformation of the people by force will be penalized, and the reformed elements and their relatives may report the facts to the county magistrate, but those who make false accusations out of malice will be punished in reverse. (9) The county magistrate of each county should announce the above-mentioned measures to the public to ensure that everyone knows them. (10) The county magistrate of each county should report the cases of resettling the coerced masses and reformed elements to the provincial government and the Department of Civil Affairs for record. Our party is very lenient to the Red bandits who repent and reform. Xu Tingyao captured thousands of bandit officials and soldiers in Huoqiu this time. Except for a few dozen important bandits who are responsible for political guidance who are temporarily detained, the rest are given funds to return to their hometowns. Seventy to eighty percent of the Red bandits are coerced or enticed, hoping that they can abandon evil and return to righteousness. Forgetfulness is indeed an inferiority of the Chinese nation. After the September 18th Incident, the people of the country only knew the danger of the Northeast and forgot the hidden danger of the Red bandits. After the January 28th Incident, the people of the country only knew the danger of Shanghai and ignored the problems of the Northeast and the Red bandits. When the Shanghai war stopped and the Japanese soldiers withdrew, the people of the country regarded resisting aggression and suppressing bandits as if they were irrelevant, living in a drunken dream, singing and dancing, and indulging in the sweet dream of the old nation for thousands of years. If this continues, even without the invasion of foreign enemies and bandits, it will be difficult for the Chinese nation to reach the path of independence, equality, and freedom. This is what I personally feel most painful about, and I hope that the people of the country will make serious corrections.

The Rampant Banditry in Wuyuan 62

Wuyuan Correspondence: Wuyuan is located on the border of Anhui, adjacent to Jiangxi and Zhejiang. In recent years, the Red bandits have caused disaster in Jiangxi, and the situation in Wuyuan has been tense from time to time. Since last winter, when Zhou Jianping and Tang Zai just two bandit groups took advantage of the withdrawal of the garrison troops in Wuyuan, they looted and burned extensively and left. Last month, Shao and Zhou two bandit groups with more than 4,000 people, besieged Xinheng in Dexing County, and at that time, they planned to attack Wuyuan City again. Fortunately, the bandit suppression army stationed in Jiangxi joined forces with the air force to launch a combined attack, killing more than 2,000 bandits. The remnants fled in all directions. It is heard that recently, hundreds of bandits from the group have fled to the area of Tian Zhanfang, 30 miles away in Dongxiang, 40 miles away from Wuyuan City, looting extensively. Many of the nearby villages that did not have time to escape were captured, and their lives and property suffered heavy losses. There is now a trend of spreading throughout the county. It is heard that the central government has dispatched the 57th Division, Tan Brigade, from Wuhu to garrison the county seat. Huabu and Kaihua on the border of Zhejiang also have troops from the 6th Division, Zhao Guantao's unit, stationed there. It is found that the two places are close to the bandit area, so the people of the county are very anxious.

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 63

Gunpoint Robbery in Niujiaobang During the Day: A gunpoint robbery occurred in Niujiaobang, Yuanmiao Temple, Suzhou City, at around 5:00 PM on the 25th. The victim was Zhou Wenbao, a clerk from the Qimen Yiyuan Wheat Shop, who was escorting 4,000 yuan in silver to the Qingtai Zhuang in front of the temple. On the way back, because he still had a balance of 50 yuan in hand, he was intimidated by a teenager holding a handgun, who robbed him of the 50 yuan in silver. The police quickly captured the teenager and found the stolen silver and a handgun. According to his confession, his name is Xia Wenhua, an employee of the Hongsheng Match Company, 20 years old, from Ningbo (external rumors that he is the nephew of Gui Minbo, the manager of the Greater China Match Company, are inaccurate). His monthly salary at the factory is 14 yuan, and the factory provides food and lodging. This theft was actually due to a marriage arranged in his hometown for next month (August), which must be completed on schedule. All of his monthly salary has been spent, and in Ningbo customs, failing to marry on schedule is considered a great shame, so he resorted to this measure. As for the source of his handgun, according to his confession, he borrowed it from the Fifth Division of the Merchant Corps because he usually had contact with people in the Fifth Division of the Merchant Corps. The police from the Second and Third Precincts immediately transferred him to the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Record of Prison Warden Transfers: On the 26th, the High Court announced that the resignation of Cheng Zhenlin, prison warden of Taixing, was approved. The vacancy was filled by transferring Jiang Zhenyuan from Nanhui. The vacancy of the prison warden of Nanhui was filled by appointing Li Yingchang. In addition, Tao Shouhe, prison warden of Liyang, was accused of being transferred to the province. The vacancy was filled by appointing Xin Jijin, and Ye Chengshu was appointed as the acting director of the detention center of this court.

Wuxi 64

Petition to Revise New Regulations on Cotton Yarn Transportation Permits: Lixin Company of this county believes that the new Cotton Yarn and Woven Product Origin/Destination Change Transportation Permit issued by the Tax Administration of the Ministry of Finance is divided into two types: Pure Weaving Factory Special Cotton Yarn Direct Woven Product Transportation Permit. There are many obstacles, and it should state the reasons to seek improvement. It roughly stated that pure weaving factories have a wide variety of product colors, which are more unsalable than plain coarse cloth, and the situation is very different. Winter goods are stored in summer, and spring goods are sold in autumn. Often, they are stored for a year and a half and cannot be sold out. Moreover, some cotton cloths woven in spring must be sold in August or September and have been stacked for half a year without any movement. If the new regulations stipulate that the period of three months expires, it will actually be too late. Moreover, the new regulations stipulate that the permit holder may report the unsold goods to the local tax authorities, who will verify that the goods match the permit and grant an extension. This is too cumbersome. Moreover, the goods that each factory transports to wholesale outlets for distribution every day must be sold at the right time and cannot be sold out at that time. In the future, when the three-month period expires, the wholesale outlets in various places will inevitably have to apply to the local tax authorities for an extension every day. Not only will merchants suffer greatly, but the government will also feel cumbersome and overwhelmed. Although pure woven products are not goods that are directly subject to tax, they are indirectly goods that bear the unified tax. They should be treated the same as cotton yarn. Once the old regulations are changed, merchants may occasionally make omissions, and penalties will follow, which will lose the government's purpose of maintaining domestic goods. Yesterday, it specially sent a public letter to the Shanghai Chinese Cotton Mill Association, requesting it to forward it to the Tax Administration of the Ministry of Finance to strive for the revision of the two types of transportation permits stipulated in the new regulations, with a validity period of one year. If the reasons for not being able to sell out after the expiration date are still reported to the local tax authorities, who will verify that the goods match the permit, an extension will be granted.

Nantong 65

Bandits Captured in Tangzha Sentenced to Death: In Tangzha Wangjia Temple, the police and bandits engaged in a fierce battle last month, capturing bandits Li Jinbiao and Xu Zhen, who were escorted to the county government for interrogation and admitted their guilt. They have now been sentenced to death and reported to the provincial government for approval and execution.

Yuzhang Warship Salvaged by Japanese: The Yuzhang warship that sank in Nantong was previously hired by the Navy Department to be salvaged by Hubei workers. After being brought out of the water, it sank back to the bottom of the river due to cable breakage, causing the project to be suspended. It is now heard that the Navy Department has changed to the Shanghai Toyo Salvage Company to undertake the work. The conditions have been negotiated and finalized, and the salvage fee is 200,000 yuan. The company has sent six Japanese staff members to Tong for surveying. After the hot summer, they will lead their employees to Tong for salvage.

Disabled Soldiers Factory to Exhibit Products: The 18th Army established a disabled soldiers vocational factory in Tong for a year. The number of military workers has increased from 100 to more than 400. The factory's work is divided into eight categories: (1) Towels; (2) Weaving Socks; (3) Weaving Cloth; (4) Chemical Crafts Manufacturing Department; (5) Leather; (6) Shoe Making; (7) Agriculture; (8) Printing. All products are for the 18th Army's own use. The director of the factory, Zhuang Mingda, has scheduled an exhibition of various products next month to entertain representatives of the armies in various provinces and regions to facilitate the promotion of military industry policies. In addition to providing accommodation for disabled and infirm officers and soldiers to learn skills, the factory will also transport active soldiers from the army to the factory to learn skills to develop life skills to enable them to make a living independently.

Gaoyou 66

Cholera is Rampant Again: Due to the recent drought in this county, cholera is rampant again. Approximately 20 people die from the disease every day. Each household has taken precautions and does not dare to buy and eat melons, fruits, and pork.

Ministry Appoints Commissioner to Shazhou to Secretly Investigate Important Cases: Yang Shinan, a commissioner sent by the Capital Garrison Command, arrived at Chunyangtang in the Fourth District of Shazhou a few days ago to secretly investigate the district headquarters of the Fourth District Security Regiment. Zhenjiang 68

Ministry of Finance Appoints New Positions: The Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance yesterday ordered Cheng Peng to be appointed as the head of the First Section of the Department, Zheng Baozi as the head of the Second Section, Lin Shaoquan as the head of the Third Section, Yi Zhenfen as the head of the Fourth Section, and Secretary Xu Shengshi to be transferred as the head of the Fifth Section. The vacancy was replaced by Li Weiyuan. In addition, Secretary Wu Longcheng and Zheng Baoxian were ordered to be inspectors.

Summoning of Wuchang Ship Smuggling Offenders: Zhang Guangyou, the main character in the Wuchang ship smuggling case, was prosecuted by the Zhenjiang Court after the case was discovered and sentenced to one year of imprisonment and a fine of 800 yuan. Lu Jinyu, who was related to the case, was sentenced to two years and one month of imprisonment. Xu Ruirui was sentenced to six months of imprisonment and a fine of 500 yuan. All refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the High Court. Because the general amnesty was imminent, the defendants in the case had not been interrogated. Now that the general amnesty order has been issued, the criminals are appropriately sentenced to reduced sentences. The Criminal Division of the Court believes that it is still necessary to continue the interrogation in order to finalize the case. Yesterday, summons were issued and the trial was scheduled to be held at 8:00 AM on August 6.

Yangzhou 69

Terrible Epidemic Spreading: The weather has been extremely hot in recent days, with the Fahrenheit reading reaching 103 degrees. Cholera or various types of similar epidemic diseases have been found in the city and suburbs, and at least a dozen people die every day. It is even worse in Shaobo. The fastest cases are beyond treatment, and death occurs within an hour. For example, the daughter-in-law who sells clothes in Guanfeng Lane and the Qiao woman from Xiaqiao Township who came to Yang to offer incense to Guanyin. One went to see a Western doctor and returned to get a salt water injection, but was already dead when she returned. The other went from the city to the mountain, but died before reaching the mountain, and was carried back in a rattan chair. Today (24th), Chen Qixiaohe from Beixiaojie had an attack of a rash at his father-in-law's house, and died halfway while being carried, and has been taken to the Western Temple for burial.

Two Jin of Noodles Leads to Two Tragic Deaths: Mei Da and his wife, disaster victims from Yangjiazhuang, Shaobo, have two young children and have no means of support and are constantly hungry. Yesterday, Mei helped work in a neighboring village, and his wife pledged two jin of noodles from a neighboring cake shop with old clothes and returned home. After leaving through the back door to find amaranth, in the blink of an eye, only a little noodles were left. Detecting that the two children had eaten it raw because they were extremely hungry, she could not help but feel sad, and secretly entered the room and hanged herself. When Mei returned and saw the situation, knowing that he could not live, he also hanged himself. The next morning, the neighbors learned about it and helped with the funeral, which was also tragic.

Pinghu 70

Epidemic Spreads and Deaths Follow: Since the epidemic spread from Shanghai to this county, an average of six or seven people die every day inside and outside the city. Recently, the Yang family in Yinyang Lane, a storyteller from Kuailewei, a certain A from Fengjing, and a Fang from Guanghua Sock Factory all died of the epidemic within two or three hours. Coffin shops have started working at night. Most of the customers in pharmacies are those who buy ten drops of water and cologne. For a time, the medicines to treat the epidemic were sold out. Pu Yangyong, a doctor at the Central Pharmacy, specially prepared 100 yuan of medicinal seedlings and offered them as preventive injections. More than 600 people have applied for injections. There are also others who are doing the same good deeds as Pu, and the number of people seeking treatment is unknown. The towns of Xindai, Xincang, and Xinmiao are more superstitious and do not seek radical treatment, and the number of deaths is even greater.

Xiaoshan 71

Eastern Township Silkworm Farmers Change to Raising Autumn Silkworms: The silkworm farmers in the eastern township failed to produce silkworm cocoons this year, and the losses are not light. Recently, the provincial government issued autumn silkworm seeds and instructed them to change to raising autumn silkworms again to make up for the shortage. County Magistrate Zhang went to the township a few days ago to make a propaganda campaign. Now the farmers are busy with field work due to the drought, and they are not fully confident in planting rice, so most of them buy autumn silkworm seeds in order to make up for the losses.

Farmland in Four Townships Suffers from Drought: There has been no rain in Xiaoshan for the past two weeks of hot weather. Most of the mountain township farmland has withered. The early rice in the southern township is lacking rain, resulting in failure to form ears and a significant reduction in harvest. The late rice in the eastern and western townships is currently being cultivated, and the water is also very busy. However, under the hot sun every day, the river water dries up more quickly. If the drought continues for another ten days, the farmland in the four townships may be difficult to bear fruit, resulting in a drought.

Page 11

Education News

Special Article 72

How Students Should Use Their Summer Vacation

(I) Wang Xiaoying

(I) The Meaning of Summer Vacation

In the very hot summer, no matter how well-equipped the classroom is, there is no way to avoid the might of the scorching heat. Especially during the noon hours every day, the high-temperature air is suffocating and makes people drowsy, unable to muster any energy. The lamplight at night is no longer friendly, and it is even more difficult to study on your own. Therefore, there is indeed a need for a short period of vacation here—summer vacation. However, the meaning of summer vacation is not to say that students' studies can be completely abandoned during the summer vacation, but only to say that in this sweltering summer, students return home from school, and the adjustment of their lives can be decided more freely.

(II) This Year's Summer Vacation

This year's summer vacation is even more worthy of our attention. The Japanese troops in Shanghai have not completely withdrawn, the volunteer army in the three northeastern provinces is also fighting the Japanese imperialism desperately under the scorching sun, and Rehe is currently alarming again. Moreover, last year's flood has not yet been recovered, and what is in front of us is a tragic and miserable "Picture of Refugees." The national crisis is like this, the people's suffering is like this, how can we be content to enjoy ourselves alone and leisurely spend our days in this summer vacation?

Moreover, more than 80% of the people in the country currently do not have the opportunity to study. There are unemployed youths everywhere. We can say that we are very lucky to be able to fight for a chance to study among tens of thousands of people. Therefore, we must not fail this opportunity, nor can we easily spend the good time of the current summer vacation.

(III) Plans for Utilizing Summer Vacation

What should we do during the summer vacation? Below I will outline a summary, and each individual can estimate the possible extent and set their own plans.

A. In terms of academic research, the first thing to mention is academic research. Of course, we must never allow our existing knowledge to disappear from our memory, and new research should also strengthen the depth of memory and transform rigid memory into an active system. In terms of research methods, two opposite paths should be taken, which are actually half of the entire research process, that is, 1. Use existing knowledge to interpret reality, and 2. Seek new theories from the investigation of reality. As for the scope of research, it can also be roughly divided into two:

(A) Regarding natural sciences, such as the study of grains and poultry, the study of storms, seasons, rain, mountain floods, ice, hail, and meteorites, the study of improved seeds and fertilizers, the study of soil, the study of pest and disease control, the study of epidemic prevention, the study of the causes of natural disasters, the study of special products and local products, etc. Everything around us can be used as materials for the study of natural sciences.

(B) Regarding social scientists, the study of the world economic panic and the Lausanne and disarmament conferences, the study of the Soviet Union's five-year plan and cultural policy, the study of Japan, the study of the Northeast problem, the study of rural economy, the study of water conservancy and water disasters, the study of customs and cultures in various places, the study of the situation in disaster areas, the study of inland transportation, and the study of student movements, etc. It is necessary to pay attention to the fact that all social phenomena have mutually influencing and mutually exciting relationships. Read newspapers and magazines daily, and investigate special accidents that occur nearby, such as suicides and robberies, to explore various causes and results, so as to understand the essence of the existing society and prepare to decide how to take the direction of promoting social welfare when we enter society in the future.

B. In terms of cultivating body and mind, young students, with the normal climate of high spirits, should also pay special attention to cultivating body and mind. Bad habits and infectious viruses are equally great enemies of society. We must strictly prevent them from combining with our body and mind.

Important News 73

Lu Hanqin Appointed as Recommended Departmental Supervisor

Nanjing, 26th Dispatch: The Ministry of Education has appointed Lu Hanqin as a recommended supervisor.

Ministry of Education Statistics on the General Situation of Civil Schools in Various Provinces and Cities

The Ministry of Education promulgated the Outline of Measures for Public Schools in January of the 18th year of the Republic of China and has repeatedly urged its implementation. Public schools in various places have sprung up and made great progress. However, when can we expect them to be popularized, how much will the number of illiterate people be reduced, and what is the situation regarding funding, teachers, and teaching? There is no practical survey. Therefore, the Ministry prepared a questionnaire in February and March of this year and instructed the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities to fill it out item by item. Currently, 25 provinces and cities have reported to the Ministry. In order to understand the implementation of public education in the country, the Ministry has compiled a comparison of the general situation of public schools in various provinces and cities as a basis for future improvement. The following is a summary of the main points explained in the statistics: (1) The estimated number of out-of-school people in various provinces and cities is approximately 224,473,253 (referring to older out-of-school people). (2) The number of illiterate people reduced in various provinces and cities is more than 1.45 million (approximately 1.5% of the total number of illiterate people). (3) The province with the largest reduction in illiterate people is Shanxi, and the provinces with the smallest reduction are Henan, Hubei, and Xinjiang. (4) The annual funding for public schools in various provinces and cities is approximately 497,000 yuan. (5) The lowest monthly salary for teachers in public schools is 2 yuan, the highest is 50 yuan, and the average is 14.3 yuan. (6) In the total of 25 districts, 23 districts have coeducational schools, 1 district has separate schools, and 1 district only accepts male students. (7) The city with the most female students is Shanghai, and the provinces with the fewest are Shandong, Rehe, and Xinjiang. (8) The lowest age of students is 7 years old, and the highest age is 61 years old. (9) The shortest study period is three months, and the longest is one year. (10) The difficulties are generally the lack of funding and talent, uneven student levels, and difficulty in enrollment.

Local News 74

Jinan University Nursing School Movement

｜Professor Sun Hanbing and Others Go to Beijing to Petition

｜Student School Protection Movement Association Established Yesterday

Firm Opposition to the Government's Abolition and Merger of the Law and Education Schools

Representatives such as He Defu Elected to Go to Beijing to Petition

Since the Executive Yuan formally passed the Ministry of Education's proposal on July 22 to abolish and merge the Law and Education Schools of National Jinan University, in addition to the Professors' Association dispatching representatives such as Sun Hanbing and Guo Yicen to Beijing to petition, the students have been particularly enthusiastic.

Students from various departments of the school mutually elected representatives and held a temporary representative assembly in the first school building on the 24th. It was immediately resolved that all students of the school would organize a Student School Protection Movement Association to carry out and realize the task of protecting the school. A date was set for yesterday (the 25th) to convene a general assembly of all students, which was also the inaugural meeting of the Student School Protection Movement Association. Yesterday (the 25th) at 8:00 AM, all students of the school gathered in the playground of the first school building. Representatives from the Suzhou Middle School Department also attended the meeting, which was officially opened under the scorching sun. The resolutions discussed and passed on that day were: (1) The association was named the National Jinan University All-Student School Protection Movement Association; (2) The organization of the association would have the general assembly as the highest authority. After the adjournment of the general assembly, the executive committee would be the highest authority. The executive committee would be divided into five departments: general affairs, organization, publicity, social interaction, and investigation. The number of executive committee members would be twenty-one, with seven alternates, jointly elected from students of the university and middle school departments. The executive committee would be responsible to the executive committee, and there would be a separate secretariat responsible to the general assembly; (3) Issue a founding declaration; (4) Dispatch representatives He Defu, Xie Shaobai, Liu Jingyin, Feng Yuzhang, and Lin Zhuguang to Beijing by express train last night (the 25th) with a petition to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education; (5) Send telegrams to national cultural institutions and major middle schools requesting assistance, and send telegrams to overseas Chinese in Nanyang and other regions for unified support.

In addition, the association has scheduled a press conference at 2:00 PM on the 27th at the China News Agency on Weihai Road in this city to announce the establishment process and recent work of the association.

Opinions of Professor Sun Hanbing and Others

Detailed Answers to Zhu's Remarks

Concrete Plans Needed for Educational Reform

A reporter from the Nanjing Dadao News Agency yesterday interviewed Sun Hanbing, Dean of the Law School of Jinan University, Guo Yicen, Dean of the Education School, and Professors Zhang Haishu and Hu Qiuyuan at the Central Hotel, asking for their opinions on the Executive Yuan's decision to abolish and merge Jinan University. The following is a record of their conversation: The government's resolution to abolish and merge Jinan University was proposed by the Minister of Education and passed by the Executive Yuan meeting. We very much agree in principle with the Executive Yuan's general order to reform education and the remarks made by Minister of Education Zhu Jiahua on reorganizing universities across the country. In particular, we fully understand the government's painstaking efforts to reform education. However, since the reform is of universities across the country, there should be a concrete plan to give the people of the country a common vision in order to achieve the effect of comprehensive planning and overall consideration, and there should be a certain standard in implementation. This is in general terms of the reform. As for Jinan University, based on the remarks made by Minister Zhu in the "Xin Jing Daily" on the 24th, we also have a few opinions: (1)

Regarding the significance and purpose of overseas Chinese education, we believe that it is not only to cultivate overseas Chinese children who return to their homeland so that they can understand the culture and customs of the motherland, but also to cultivate talents in the country to develop overseas. We believe that the latter is more important than the former. Based on this point, we believe that Minister Zhu's so-called "someone" saying "overseas Chinese universities are unnecessary" is not necessarily reasonable, and it is not wrong for Jinan University to accept students who are not overseas Chinese children. As for saying that the purpose of establishing Jinan University is to reward overseas Chinese who have served the motherland, the original reason for its establishment may have been this, but now its purpose and significance should conform to the needs of the times and be more progressive. (2) Regarding the abolition and merger of the Law and Education Schools, in Minister Zhu's view, Jinan University should tighten its belt due to the losses suffered in the Shanghai war. As for the austerity measures, the Law School will be merged into Zhongda, and the Education School will be reduced to a department (originally three departments). We believe that there are several misunderstandings in the reasons listed in the remarks. First, university students studying education are not only preparing to become teachers. Second, we believe that the employment problem of students specializing in education is the problem of the entire education field, which cannot be solved by reducing the school to a department. Furthermore, the significance of establishing the Education School is due to the development of modern educational science. Fields such as educational administration and educational psychology have become research systems, which cannot be covered by a single department. In terms of our country's needs, it is even more necessary to value educational science, because the bankruptcy of education is a problem of the entire society. However, the lack of educational administration talents and the ignorance of educational methods are also a major reason. Regarding the Law School, our opinions are also slightly different from Minister Zhu's. First, Minister Zhu said that the National Government is located in Nanjing, and the implementation of politics originates from here. We are not sure what relationship this has with the merger of the Law School and dare not speculate. University education is not entirely limited to applied fields, but is more important for the creation of specialized scholars. For example, taking the economics department, it seems better to be located in Shanghai, the financial center of the country, than in the capital. Famous jurists and lawyers also live in Shanghai more often, so whether the Law School should be located in the capital is quite questionable. In terms of the principle of abolition and merger, according to Minister Zhu, departments and schools that overlap in the same region should be merged, but the result is exactly the opposite. There is no Education School or Law School in Shanghai National University other than Jinan University. On the contrary, Jinan University already has a well-established Business School, but now a new independent Business School has been established in Shanghai, which is not a duplication. As for saying that Jinan University must adopt a policy of austerity and concentration in order to ensure educational efficiency, what does "middle" mean? How to "concentrate"? The remarks did not explain. Looking at the effect of austerity from the perspective of funding, it is also questionable. Jinan University can certainly save money by tightening its belt, but wouldn't Zhongda have to increase because of expansion? Furthermore, although the Law and Education Schools of Jinan University are abolished and merged, the basic subjects of the two schools, such as political economy and other social sciences, as well as psychology and teaching methods, still need to be established and still require considerable funding. In addition, there is one more point, that is, such a major reform of a university must be discussed with the school authorities in advance. If the school's plan for the coming year is gradually implemented, and then it is suddenly greatly changed, then the fact is that it is very difficult. Jinan University's enrollment is about to close, and the letters of appointment for next year's professors have already been issued. This kind of disregard for practical difficulties seems to be insufficient to show respect for education and the intention to reform education. We are sincerely supportive of the government's and Minister Zhu's intention to reform education, but we hope that on the one hand, we will work hard to reform, and on the other hand, we should also consider the actual situation. We hope that Jinan University can take into account the facts of the school and properly plan a good solution.

Summary of the Performance Evaluation of Municipal Schools in the 20th Year

(Central News Agency) The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education is required to conduct an annual assessment of the performance of municipal school principals at the end of the academic year. According to the results of this year's assessment, among the city's more than 180 schools, those whose terms have expired and should be reappointed are: 17 schools whose first phase of one-year service has expired, and 14 schools whose second phase of two-year service has expired. Specifically, with the exception of the South District, there are no changes in the municipal primary schools in the Shanghai South District. Ruan Xingzhi, the principal of the South District Primary School, has repeatedly requested to resign last year, but the Education Bureau has instructed him to stay. Now the principal has resolutely resigned, and Director Xu of the Education Bureau has failed to persuade him to stay and has approved his resignation. He has selected Cheng Minkai, the principal of Zhenxiu Primary School, who has worked hard in school management, to be transferred to the South District. Chen Xiangxin, the principal of Wusong Primary School, has been transferred to Zhenxiu, and Chen Liqing, the principal of Yinxie Primary School, has been transferred to Wusong. Chen Shouzhi, the principal of Gaoqiao Primary School, has been transferred to Yinxie, Su Shude, the principal of Tangyan Primary School, has been transferred to Gaoqiao, and Jin Xuanlun, the principal of Gucun Primary School, has been transferred to Tangyan. Most of them are promotions. The principal of Gucun Primary School will be replaced by a qualified person appointed by the Education Bureau. Regarding the municipal schools in Zhabei District, temporary primary schools have been newly established in accordance with the temporary reorganization plan after the January 28th Incident. The principals have been appointed to be responsible for the reorganization and opening of the schools. Regarding the municipal schools in rural areas, Zhao Tizhen, the principal of Jincheng Primary School, has resigned and has been replaced by Shi Hengsheng, the principal of Xigou Primary School. In addition, principals of various primary schools in rural areas have been dismissed for poor management, ineffective school management, or dereliction of duty, or for gambling. There are 11 schools in total, most of which are single-grade primary schools. The Education Bureau has appointed qualified personnel to replace them. There are also several schools that have been mutually transferred. New Plan for the First Municipal Experimental Primary School

Jia Yin Appointed Principal

The Shanghai First Municipal Experimental Primary School is one of the educational experimental institutions specially established by the Municipal Bureau of Education. Therefore, the Bureau of Education attaches great importance to it, and the Ministry of Education also pays close attention to it. The school's experiments in the past few years have focused on gifted children. However, this is an initiative in educational experiments in various countries, and the results obtained have not yet been determined. The Bureau plans to formulate a new plan for the coming year, expand the scope of the experiment, and pay attention to the selection of principals. Special standards have been set, and only those with the following qualifications can be appointed: (1) Must have graduated from a university education department or a higher normal school and have received higher education training; (2) Must have been in charge of an experimental primary school for more than three years and have achieved results; (3) Must have insights and writings on primary school education and be rich in educational research. It has now been decided to select Jia Yin as the principal. Mr. Jia graduated from the Education Department of National Higher Normal School and has served as the director of the Taicang Education Bureau, the director of moral education of Jiangsu Provincial Fourth Middle School, the director of the affiliated primary school of the Education Department, the principal of the experimental primary school of Jiangsu Provincial Taicang Middle School, the secretary of the Fujian Education Department, the director of the primary education department, the local education guidance, and a teacher and lecturer at the Fujian Local Administrative Personnel Class A Training Institute. He has rich experience and writings. He has written 22 books, 18 papers, and 3 translations, which meet the above standards very well. The Municipal Bureau of Education has already appointed him. It is reported that Mr. Jia has come to Shanghai to take over.

Minister of Finance Song Flew to Beijing Yesterday Morning 79

Zhang Xueliang's Advisor, Dana, Accompanying

According to the Central News Agency, Minister of Finance Song Ziwen came to Shanghai this time to confer with important personnel from the customs and taxation departments and various financial circles on how to deal with the rebellion seizing customs duties in the Northeast, discuss methods for abolishing the tael and replacing it with the yuan, and plan for the increase of 1.5 million yuan in the anti-banditry funds that were previously discussed with President Wang in Shanghai. Most of the important issues have been settled, so Mr. Song took Mr. Zhang's private plane to Beijing at 5:15 AM yesterday morning, accompanied by Zhang Xueliang's advisor, Dana, and others. The matters discussed by Mr. Song with various circles in the city before leaving Shanghai and the circumstances of his departure are recorded below:

Important Meetings Held Before Leaving Shanghai After Mr. Song came to Shanghai this time, he held meetings for several days with Vice Minister of Finance Zhang Shouyong, Jianghai Customs Supervisor Tang Haian, Chief Inspector of Customs Meierhe, Director of the Customs Affairs Department Zhang Fuyun, Chinese and foreign advisors from the customs and taxation departments, and financial circles such as Yu Qiaqing, Bei Songsun, Li Fusun, and Hu Mengjia to discuss customs duties, the abolition of the tael and the replacement of the yuan, and various important financial issues, all of which have yielded considerable results. At about 9:30 PM the night before last, Mr. Song and others held another important meeting at the Chief Inspector of Customs Office on Hart Road. Those present included Zhang Shouyong, Meierhe, Zhang Fuyun, Tang Haian, and western advisor Yang Ge and other eight people. According to the results of the meeting, it is said that some important principles have been decided. A reporter from the Central News Agency interviewed Chief Inspector of Customs Meierhe yesterday to inquire about the course of the meeting. Because Meierhe did not want to publish anything about this, he asked various parties for information on how to deal with the problem of the rebellion seizing customs duties in the Northeast. It was decided to blockade the Northeast customs and publish a declaration on the blockade of the customs in the three northeastern provinces. As for the various measures to be taken after the blockade of the Northeast customs, specific measures have also been drafted. Due to his eagerness to leave Shanghai, Mr. Song has temporarily handed over the tasks of Shanghai negotiations to Vice Minister of Finance Zhang Shouyong to carry out separately, so as to implement them in the near future.

After Arriving in Beijing, He Will Go to Wuhan and Then to Peiping Because Zhang Xueliang, the Pacification Commissioner of Peiping, is very concerned about the Japanese army's ambition to attack Rehe and because the rebellion's seizure of customs is urgent, he specially sent his Western advisor, Dana, on Zhang's private plane from Beijing to Shanghai the night before last. After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Dana immediately met with Mr. Song to report on everything and was ordered to invite Mr. Song to go north to discuss matters. Therefore, Mr. Song took the original plane to Beijing at 5:15 AM yesterday morning. In addition to Zhang's advisor Dana, Qin and Chen's secretaries and Shen Qingyi, an advisor to the Ministry of Finance, also accompanied him. After arriving in Beijing, Mr. Song will visit President Wang to report on everything and will then take the original plane to Wuhan to visit Chiang and then go north to visit Zhang.

News from Outside the Pass: Suspension of Postal Services 80

Original Bureau for Refund of Three Provinces Drafts

Faster Postal Routes Available in Southeast Asia

Following the government's order to block postal services in the Northeast, postal services in the three provinces have been terminated, and all personnel are entering the Pass in succession. The following is a record of yesterday's news:

Shanghai Postal Bureau News: Regarding the suspension of postal services in the three northeastern provinces, a notice was issued on Sunday (the 24th), announcing the complete suspension of drafts issued by the bureaus in those three provinces, parcels sent to those provinces, and all other postal items. The public is further reminded that drafts issued by those bureaus will no longer be honored. The original payment amount should be claimed directly from the issuing bureau by the purchaser. Furthermore, mail transported via Siberia should (unless otherwise notified) be rerouted via the Pacific Ocean or the Suez Canal.

Lin Shi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning: Lin Shi, Director of the Postal Department of the Ministry of Communications, has been making great efforts to deal with the situation since the rebels seized postal services in the Northeast. After the Ministry of Communications announced the blockade of postal services in the Northeast on the 23rd of this month, he arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning, as Shanghai is the national postal center. After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Lin met with Huang Naishu, Director-General of Posts, to conduct a thorough study of the various measures to be taken after the blockade of postal services in the Northeast, and has drafted a number of concrete plans.

Mr. Liu Yaoting's Remarks: According to the Datong News Agency, Liu Yaoting, Deputy Postal Director of the Shenyang Postal Bureau in the Liaoning area, paid a visit to Huang Naishu, Director-General of Posts, after arriving in Shanghai, to report on the events leading up to the blockade of postal services in the Northeast and the arrangements for postal workers to enter the Pass in batches, providing a detailed account. However, Mr. Liu, deeply affected by the difficulties he faced in Shenyang, and exhausted from the journey, is now suffering from dysentery. He has been granted leave by the General Bureau for temporary recuperation. A Datong News Agency reporter met with him at his residence yesterday. According to Mr. Liu, he took a train from Shenyang on the morning of the 16th and stayed briefly in Beijing and Tianjin to coordinate arrangements for postal workers entering the Pass. He arrived in Shanghai on the afternoon of the 24th (Sunday). He added that he could not disclose the current situation of postal services in the Northeast at this time, but it was generally the same as reported in the newspapers. At the time, a senior official from the Shanghai Postal Bureau was also present and made two points to the reporter: (1) There are more than 30,000 postal workers nationwide, but only over 2,000 in the Northeast. The report that there are over 30,000 postal workers in the Northeast is incorrect. (2) The Postal Director of Shenyang, Mr. Balidi, and the Postal Director of Harbin, Mr. Sismis, will only begin their journey into the Pass after all postal workers from the Northeast have entered the Pass. They are currently still in their respective bureaus, handling the final arrangements. The reporter also learned that Mr. Liu is from Henan Province and was appointed as Deputy Postal Director of Shenyang in the autumn of the 18th year of the Republic of China, having stayed in Shenyang for more than three years. His family was also in Shenyang but have since followed Mr. Liu to safety in Beijing.

Postal Workers Gather in Four Locations: Postal workers from the three provinces are entering the Pass on orders, but not as a single unit. Instead, travel expenses are issued by each postal bureau, instructing them to travel separately to four locations: Beijing, Tianjin, Qingdao, and Shanghai. The bureau also provides travel expenses for reaching one of these four locations. As of yesterday, the General Bureau had not received reports on how many of the approximately two thousand postal workers from outside the Pass would be assigned to Shanghai.

Glimpse of the Postal Union Regulations: Regarding the Japanese government's introduction of the puppet Manchukuo to join the Universal Postal Union, a person in charge of the General Postal Bureau stated that, according to the regulations of the Postal Union, joining the Union requires the introduction of three member states. As only Japan is acting as the introducer, this does not fully comply with the regulations. Without joining the Postal Union, not only would its issued stamps be equivalent to invalid stamps according to regulations, but it would also be fundamentally unable to qualify for exchanging mail with member states.

Faster Postal Route in Southeast Asia: According to the "North China Daily News,"

Since the blockade of postal services in the Northeast, mail to Europe has been rerouted by sea, which takes several days longer than taking the Siberian route. However, there is an even faster postal route than the Siberian route that may not be well known to the public. The Netherlands has recently opened a regular air route between Batavia (Java) and Amsterdam. Light mail, such as letters, sent from Shanghai via this route can reach Europe in 18 days. The connecting method is to send the mail by ship to Java or Singapore, and then connect with the Dutch air route in Batavia or Alorstar. The Batavia-Amsterdam air route is one of the longest air routes in the world and has been operating for several years, but it is little known in China. Its history dates back to 1924 when a Dutch aviator flew a single-engine plane from Amsterdam to Batavia, encountering several obstacles along the way and arriving in 24 days. Three years later, the famous Dutch aviator Koopman flew again, this time in a three-engine plane, and completed the journey smoothly from the Netherlands to Java in just 12 days, and the return journey was even faster, taking only nine days, setting a new world record at the time. In 1931, this record was broken. Subsequently, a subsidiary company was established in Java, named the Dutch East Indies Airlines, with four aircraft. After a third test flight on November 1, 1929, regular flights began, operating every 14 days, carrying passengers and mail. At the time, the Dutch postal authorities, to facilitate the public, provided very light airmail stationery and envelopes and charged very low airmail rates, but only for light mail. Parcels and heavy mail still had to be transported by sea. On October 1, 1930, the service was changed to once a week to facilitate transportation, which almost doubled the amount of mail carried. The flight time has also been shortened, with Batavia to Amsterdam taking only nine days, and the flights are very stable. In the three years since its opening, there has only been one incident, and the mail was not damaged, only delayed by five days. Currently, flights depart from Amsterdam every Thursday and arrive in Batavia the following Friday, and depart from Batavia every Friday and arrive in Amsterdam the following Saturday. Recently, the company plans to use new aircraft to shorten the flight time, hoping to reach the destination in five days. As for the connection between China and this air route, a Hong Kong-Singapore air route could be opened to connect directly with Java, and if it were extended further north to Xiamen and Shanghai, mail sent from Shanghai could reach Europe in at most ten days in the future.

Japanese Residents to Mail to Northeast 81

Acceptance to Begin Today

Mailboxes Added at the Bund Wharf

Japanese Ships to Dalian to Sail Every Three Days

Since our blockade of the postal bureaus in the Eastern Provinces, Japanese residents in Shanghai have been extremely panicked and have been discussing countermeasures for days, planning to first organize a temporary postal bureau to deal with the situation. Although the spokesperson of the Japanese Consulate has repeatedly denied this, the Japanese residents still held a meeting yesterday to discuss solutions. Our authorities believe that such actions by the Japanese residents would be illegal, so they have dispatched personnel to investigate secretly. The details are recorded below:

Yesterday's Meeting of Japanese Residents: According to the Far East News Agency, in order to establish a temporary communication mechanism with the puppet Manchukuo in the future, and to counter our blockade policy, the Japanese residents of this port have been holding meetings for several days. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m., the acting chairman of the administrative committee of the Japanese Residents' Association, Yasui, the chairmen of the various chambers of commerce, Lin Xiongji, and members of the Current Affairs Association, etc., convened a meeting at the Japanese Club to discuss the matter. The meeting did not end until 6:00 p.m. According to Japanese newspaper reporters, a concrete plan has been decided as a result of the meeting, roughly deciding to set up a transportation agency to accept letters to Manchuria. In name, they will try to avoid names such as "postal bureau" so as not to conflict with international law and the Universal Postal Union. This agency will be located in the Japanese Club or the General Assembly of the Residents' Association, and personnel who previously worked in the Japanese Residents' Postal Bureau in this port during the strike of our postal workers will be hired to handle all mailing work, so as to ensure familiarity, and efforts will be made to transfer several postal workers from Japan to assist. The responsibility for transporting the letters will be borne by the Dalian Steamship Company and the Shanghai branch of Nippon Yusen Kaisha. They will also maintain close contact with Japanese residents in Tianjin and Dalian, and have already sent telegrams to solicit methods and opinions from both places. It is said that they will also send personnel north to make contact if necessary.

Dalian Ships Handle Delivery on Behalf: This newspaper reporter has learned that the collection and delivery of mail to the Northeast and Siberia by the Japanese has been confirmed as of yesterday, and will be handled by the Shanghai-bound ships of the Dalian Steamship Company, which is run by the South Manchuria Railway. It is stipulated that Shanghai can send and receive every three days. Secondly, yesterday the Dalian Steamship Company received a telegram from its headquarters, instructing that the mail room on the ship be enlarged starting from today's departing ship, and a special commissioner be appointed to manage postal affairs.

Mailboxes Set Up at the Wharf: Yesterday, the Dalian Steamship Company added mailboxes on the Bund wharf, specifically for mailing mail to places such as the three northeastern provinces, Harbin, and Siberia. The establishment of a postal bureau may cause international disputes, so a person has been specially dispatched to the wharf to be responsible for collecting letters, in effect having a postal bureau without the name of one. In terms of procedures, it is taking a shortcut.

Acceptance to Begin Today: The Japanese will begin collecting mail to the Northeast from 8:00 a.m. today at the Bund wharf. It is said that the postage for mail to Siberia was originally set at 25 cents per ounce, but is now reduced to 14 cents, and no stamps will be affixed. Instead, a stamp will be applied by the collection office. Yesterday, many people went to the Dalian Steamship Company on Sichuan Road to mail letters to the Northeast. In addition to instructing them to go to the Bund wharf to deliver them, the company issued a notice stating that the company does not accept letters to the three northeastern provinces, etc. The first batch of mail collected on behalf of the company today will be delivered to Dalian tomorrow morning at 9:00 a.m. by the Dalian Maru ship, and then forwarded to various places in the three northeastern provinces, Harbin, and Siberia.

Provisional Delivery Method Set: Currently, it is provisionally stipulated that postal services to the Northeast can be provided every three days. Secondly, they will not be collected and delivered every day, but will be collected and delivered one day on the morning after the Dalian Steamship arrives in Shanghai. The second batch of letters to the Northeast will be collected on the 31st and sent out on August 1st by the Fengtian Maru ship. As for mail from various places in the Northeast to Shanghai, it will also be carried by the company's ships and then forwarded by personnel.

Visa Manifests for Goods Transported to China from Overseas Consulates 82

To Be Implemented from September 1st

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, noting that there are no consular visa manifests for imported foreign goods, has submitted a request to the National Government to implement the issuance of visa manifests by overseas consulates, and has stipulated 14 articles of regulations, which will be implemented from September 1st. The regulations are recorded below: Article 1: From the date of implementation of these regulations, all goods transported to China from overseas, with a value of more than 200 national currency units, except for postal packages and goods exempted from customs duties, must be accompanied by a consular visa manifest issued by the Chinese consulate stationed at or near the place of export. Article 2: The consular visa manifest referred to in the preceding article can be obtained from the nearest Chinese consulate. The merchant must fill in each item in detail and have it signed by the person in charge before submitting it to the Chinese consulate stationed at or near the place of export for visa. Article 3: The consul shall verify the items filled in the manifest to ensure their accuracy before issuing the visa. If it is deemed necessary to verify the documents or other documents, the merchant shall comply. Article 4: The consular visa manifest is issued in triplicate, one original, which is white, and two copies, which are yellow. The original copy is given to the merchant by the consulate that issued the consular visa manifest to be forwarded to the consignee for customs inspection. The other two copies, one is kept by the consulate, and the other is sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs monthly. Article 5: A handling fee of five customs gold units is charged for each set of consular visa manifests, and is collected at the time of issuance. Article 6: The consular visa fees collected by the consul shall be remitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs monthly along with the consular visa manifest copies. Article 7: If goods are sold to two importing merchants, or packed into two merchant ships, or imported to two ports, they must not be declared on the same manifest. Article 8: After the goods arrive at their destination, the consignee shall submit the original of the visa manifest to the customs for verification when declaring customs. Article 9: If imported goods do not have a consular visa manifest, the consignee shall pay three times the prescribed visa fee as a fine, and the goods shall be released after the customs office reissues the visa manifest. Article 10: At the end of each month, the customs office shall list the visa manifests collected and the amount of fines, and report them to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and send the manifests and fines to the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance. Article 11: The gold unit of customs shall be collected by the consulates in accordance with the exchange rates of various currencies announced by the customs, as ordered by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Article 12: The consular visa manifests shall be printed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stamped, and issued to the consulates and customs offices for use. Article 13: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be submitted for amendment at any time. Article 14: These regulations shall be implemented from September 1, 21st year of the Republic of China.

Rice Industry Pays Attention to Foreign Rice 90

Investigating Goods Continuously Transported by Japanese Merchants

The supply of foreign rice in Shanghai has been crowded this year, but sales are sluggish, and market prices are gradually declining. The price of small twisted rice has fallen to 8.67 yuan, but the sales path remains stagnant. There are currently more than 1.6 million bags of rice stored in various warehouses. Due to the hot weather, the rice is piled up and not moving, with some stored in warehouses for five, six, eight, or nine months. It is feared that if it is not sold for a long time, it will become moldy. Therefore, various warehouses are informing the owners to take the goods. Among the rice stored in various warehouses, half is rice transported by Japanese merchants. Upon learning of this, the rice industry association immediately refused to buy and sell it, and the association held a meeting to discuss measures to crack down on inferior goods. Fearing that the members would secretly trade with them, the association has warned all members. However, Japanese merchants secretly entrusted brokers to sell the rice, promising high profits and reducing the price to 8.1 yuan. Recently, certain firms in the Wanyu Wharf in Nanshi have bought the rice at this price, hoping to make a profit by selling it. The matter was heard by the industry, and the firms were advised not to buy inferior goods. The association has held a meeting to break off economic ties with Japan, and our members must not violate this and must abide by the resolutions. On the one hand, they are investigating the brokers who handled the transactions and the amount of goods in order to report to the association for disposal.

The Municipal Bureau of Public Works Actively Constructs the Gaoqiao East Embankment 95

Construction Completed, No Worries for the Autumn Floods

The sea embankment in the Gaoqiao East Embankment area of this city suffered from strong winds and heavy rains last autumn, which eroded and damaged the sea embankment. At that time, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works sent personnel to repair it as a temporary expedient. This year, the Bureau of Public Works, in view of the dangerous situation last year, is taking precautions and making long-term plans. Bidding began on June 1st, and construction started on June 6th, divided into nine sections. Seven sections from the "Ai" section to the "Qiang" section were completely rebuilt as stone embankments. The "Rong" section to the "Xia Er" section, which were originally concrete embankments, have also been repaired. The nine sections total 1,700 meters, 11,100 cubic meters, and the total cost is 550,000 yuan. The municipal government has now allocated 250,000 yuan, and the remaining funds will be allocated by the Embankment Works Committee and other sources. The plan is to complete the rebuilt stone embankments in seven phases and the repaired embankments in five phases. It is expected that all will be completed in one month. Although the Public Works personnel are scorched by the sun, their work has not been interrupted, and half of the work has already been completed. If the rain does not cause any hindrance, it will be possible to complete all the work according to the steps. According to the Bureau of Public Works, if this project is done well, there will be no worries about the autumn floods this year.

This kind of overestimation of rent and tax collection is illegal and unreasonable, and it is infuriating. We demand negotiations to return the extra money in full in order to demonstrate justice. The 16th joint meeting resolved to send a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association to strongly protest and punish the tax collectors in order to maintain the credibility of the Public Works Bureau,' etc. The overestimation of rent and tax collection will unduly increase the burden on taxpayers. If this is not stopped, the consequences will be dire. We are responding to the situation by requesting that your association seriously negotiate to prevent this illegal tax collection from happening again in order to avoid many disputes,' etc. The overestimation of rent and tax collection is actually the same as increasing the tax rate. This association has repeatedly sent letters to your bureau to correct this, but it has repeatedly occurred, which is regrettable. In response to the aforementioned letter, we are writing to request that your bureau order the tax office to refund the overcollected 6 taels, 8 qian, and 6 fen to Dexintang. Sincerely, to the Director-General of the Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Bureau."

And Designation of Yin Rugeng as Chairman

The organizational rules of the Municipal Police Administration Reorganization Committee have been announced by the municipal government. As for the selection of committee members, Mayor Wu has carefully considered and finalized them yesterday, appointing Wen Yingxing, Yin Rugeng, Luo Jingyi, He Ganlu, Kui, Jin Gong, Liang Fuchu, Wang Zhijing, and Ma Hongru, and designating Yin Rugeng as the chairman.

The Emei Steamboat Escapes Danger 99

Passengers, Crew, and Cargo are All Safe

Only the Left Keel is Slightly Damaged and Has Been Repaired

The Emei steamboat of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which operates between Chongqing and Yichang, captained by Ji Qingrong and first officer Li Yunheng, departed from Chongqing fully loaded with cargo and passengers on the morning of the 21st of this month for Yichang. At about 1:00 PM, it ran aground at Lianzhu Dam. The ship was unable to move. Yesterday, the Shanghai General Bureau received a telegram stating that the Emei steamboat escaped danger after running aground for more than 30 minutes. Passengers, crew, and cargo were all completely safe. It has now arrived safely in Yichang. After unloading passengers and cargo, workers were sent to inspect and found that several places such as the iron pillar platform in the left keel of the second cargo hold were slightly damaged. They immediately hired workers to repair them and have restored them to their original condition and are operating normally.
